[The server did not respond to the connection attempt within a reasonable time, it may be temporarily down. Try again later.]
服务器并未在可接受的时间内回应连接尝试，它可能暂时停机。请稍候再试。
[The connection with the server was abortively closed during the connection attempt. You may have lost your local network connection.]
与服务器的连接在尝试连接时被放弃式关闭。您可能已失去局域网连接。
[Miranda was unable to resolve the name of a server to its numeric address. This is most likely caused by a catastrophic loss of your network connection (for example, your modem has disconnected), but if you are behind a proxy, you may need to use the 'Resolve hostnames through proxy' option in M->Options->Network.]
Miranda 无法将服务器名称解析成数字式地址。这通常是由放突然失去网络连接 (例如，您的调制解调器已断线) 所导致的，但如果您是在代理服务器后面，您就可能需要使用在 M→选项→网络中的“透过代理服务器解析主机名称”选项。
[Miranda was unable to make a connection with a server. It is likely that the server is down, in which case you should wait for a while and try again later.]
Miranda 无法与服务器创建连接。这可能是服务器不可用，若是这样请等候一会，然后再试一次。
[Your proxy rejected the user name and password that you provided. Please check them in M->Options->Network.]
您的代理服务器已经拒绝您所输入的用户名及密码。请在“M->选项->网络”中作出检查。
[The server to which you are trying to connect does not exist. Check your spelling in M->Options->Network->ICQ.]
您正尝试连接到的服务器并不存在。请在“M->选项->网络->ICQ”中检查您的拼写。

[When the Individual Sounds page gets opened, you can:]
当打开个别声音页后，您可以：

- 藉选择状态并点选“删除”或按下 DEL 键就可以删除声音。当您删除声音后，将使用默认的声音。

[MUST start with line() followed by a number or a string inside " marks, OR csv(seperatorX) variable\r\n]
必须以 line() 以及一数目或在 " 标记内的字符串，或 csv(分隔符X) 变量\r\n
[The number specifies which character in the line to start/end copying.\r\nThe string specifies a string in the line to start/end copying.\r\n]
该数目指定在句子中要开始/退出复制的字符。\r\n字符串则指定在句子中要开始/退出复制的文字。\r\n
[csv(seperatorX) explained...\r\nseperator is either "tab" or "space" or any SINGLE character.\r\nX is the Xth seperator to pass before copying, (or to stop before)\r\n\r\n]
csv(分隔符X) 的讲解...\r\n分隔符可以是 "tab" 或 "space" 或任何单一字符。\r\nX 是在复制前先越过的第 X 个分隔符 (或在停止前)\r\n\r\n
[Lastly the line(...) variable...\r\n]
最后是 line(...) 变量...\r\n
[Inside the brackets must be either a number (to specify the line number), or a string inside " marks (to use the line with that string), or lastline(X).\r\nthe X in lastline is the Xth line above the last line. i.e lastline(1) will use the 2nd last line of the file.\r\n]
在括号内必须是数目 (指定行号)，或在 " 标记内的字符串 (使用在字符串的句子)，或 lastline(X)。\r\nlastline 的 X 是最后一行对上的第 X 行。例如 lastline(1) 将使用文件的最后第 2 行。\r\n
[If searching for a line with u may put a + or - X after the closing ) i.e line("some words")+3 to go 3 lines after the line with "some words".\r\n\r\n]
如果在句子中进行搜索，您可以在关闭的 ) 后加上 + 或 - X，即是 line("一些字词")+3 前进到含 "一些字词" 句子的后 3 行。\r\n\r\n
[Some Expamples...\r\n\r\n]
一些例子...\r\n\r\n
[filename(0)     <- will display the filename of the 0th file\r\nfile(0)wholeline(line(0))) <- will display the whole first line of the 0th file\r\nfile(0)wholeline(line("hello")-1))) <- the wholeline above the first occurance of "hello" in the file\r\nfile(0)start(line(lastline(1))csv(tab2))end(line(lastline())csv(tab4))) <- starts at the 2nd last line of the file, from the 2nd tab variable, untill the 4th tab variable in the last line (in the 0th file)\r\nfile(0)start(line("hello")+1"zzzz")end(line(6)17)) <- starts from the first occurance of zzzz in the line after the first occurance of hello, untill the 17th character in the 6th line (starting from line 0) of the 0th file.\r\n]
filename(0)     <- 将显示第 0 个文件的文件名\r\nfile(0)wholeline(line(0))) <- 将显示第 0 个文件第一行的整行\r\nfile(0)wholeline(line("您好")-1))) <- wholeline 应用于文件内第一个出现 "您好" 的句子\r\nfile(0)start(line(lastline(1))csv(tab2))end(line(lastline())csv(tab4))) <- 开始于文件的最后第 2 行，由第 2 个分栏变量开始，直至最后一行的第 4 个分栏变量 (在第 0 个文件)\r\nfile(0)start(line("hello")+1"zzzz")end(line(6)17)) <- 由第 0 个文件中第一个出现您好的句子后面出现第一个 zzzz 的行开始，直至第 6 行的第 17 个字符 (由第 0 行开始)。\r\n

[With Web Miranda Configurator, you can customize the settings for both Web Miranda, and the original Miranda client.]
有了 Web Miranda 设置程序，您可以自定义 Web Miranda 及 Miranda 软件的设置。
[You can make your own plugin page which will be shown in the list on the left, open sample.misc.php in config directory for more information.]
您可以制作您自己的插件页面，而它会被显示于左方的列表。若要更多消息，请打开 config 目录中的 sample.misc.php。
[Configurator Security Status:]
设置程序安全性状态：
[You currently have full access to all configuration settings]
您当前可对所有设置项目有完整访问权
[You currently have read-only access to configuration options. Please use your administrator credentials to unlock.]
您当前对所有设置项目有只读访问权。请使用您的管理员凭证消息解除锁定。

[User Password]
用户密码
[If you want to be asked for password when starting Web Miranda!, assign a username and password here.]
如果您想在启动 Web Miranda! 时被询问密码，请在这里分配用户名及密码。
[NOTE: The user password can be overridden by the Administrator Password.]
注意：用户密码可由管理员密码所取替。
[<u>N</u>o Password]
没有密码(<u>N</u>)
[<u>E</u>nable authentication with]
启动凭证(<u>E</u>)，使用
[Administrator Password]
管理员密码
[If you want to protect the Web Miranda Configurator with password, assign them here.]
如果您想以密码保护 Web Miranda 设置程序，请在这里分配。
[NOTE: If you forget the Administrator Password, you will have no way to change anything here unless you reset it by deleting the value using Miranda's Database Editor plugin.]
注意：如果您忘记了管理员密码，您将没有方法更改这里的内容，除非您使用 Miranda 的数据库编辑器插件把设置数值删掉。
[<u>S</u>ame as User Password/No Password]
与用户密码相同/没有密码(<u>S</u>)
[En<u>a</u>ble authentication with]
启动凭证(<u>a</u>)，使用

[Padding is the additional space between the tab label or icon and the tab border.\nThe inner margin defines the spacing between the tab page and its contents while the outer margin defines the spacing between the tab page and the container window border.]
补位是在分页标签与分方案线间所附加的空位。\n内部边界定义分页与它的内容间的空位，而外部边界定义分页与集中器的窗口框线间的空位。

[ Notes ]
注释
[  Refresh time (sec) is time to refresh music info and status messages. If zero, automatic refresh is disabled.\n  Only if 'Music' status was set - change your status if Music XStatus sets already.\n  Keep 'Music' XStatus - if player stopped or shutdowned, save or not 'Music' XStatus (changes to empty).\n  If text after processing is empty, the status message does not changes.\n  If settings saved in ini-file, its will be deleted from Miranda DB. Else ini-file will be deleted.]
刷新时间(秒) - 刷新音乐消息和状态消息的时间。设成零则不自动刷新。 \n 仅当'音乐'状态被设置 - 若音乐的X状态已设置则改变你的状态。 \n  保持'音乐'的X状态 - 若播放器停止或改变时，保存或者非'音乐' \n X状态(变成空)。若在处理后的文本为空，则状态消息不变。 \n  把设置保存在INI配置文件 - 选中后将从Miranda的数据库中删除配置消息，否则ini文件将被删除。

[Quick Quide to Regular Expressions:]
正规表示式的快速导航：
[Alternatives:]
互换方式：
[gilbert|sullivan finds "gilbert" or "sullivan"]
gilbert|sullivan 寻找 "gilbert" 或 "sullivan"
[Subpatterns:]
子式样：
[cat(aract|erpillar) finds "cataract" or "caterpillar"]
cat(aract|erpillar) 寻找 "cataract" 或 "caterpillar"
[Repetitions:]
重复：
[z{2,4} matches "zz", "zzz" or "zzzz"\r\n* is equivalent to {0,}\r\n+ is equivalent to {1,}\r\n? is equivalent to {0,1}]
z{2,4} 符合 "zz"、"zzz" 或 "zzzz"\r\n* 等同于 {0,}\r\n+ 等同于 {1,}\r\n? 等同于 {0,1}
[Generic Types:]
一般类型：
[\\d represents any decimal digit\r\n\\D represents any character that is not a decimal digit]
\\d 代表任何十进位数字\r\n\\D 代表任何不是十进位数字的字节
[Assertions:]
测试：
[(?<!foo)bar finds an occurrence of "bar" that is not preceded by "foo"\r\n(?<= for positive lookahead assertions\r\n(?<! for negative lookahead assertions\r\n(?= for positive lookbehind assertions\r\n(?! for negative lookbehind assertions]
(?<!foo)bar 寻找没有 "foo" 开头的 "bar"\r\n(?<= 正值前向查找\r\n?<! 负值前向查找\r\n(?= 正值后向查找\r\n(?! 负值后向查找
[Back References:]
反向参照：
[(sens|respons)e and \\1ibility matches "sense and sensibility" and "response and responsibility", but not "sense and responsibility"]
(sens|respons)e and \\1ibility 符合 "sense and sensibility" 及 "response and responsibility"，但不符合 "sense and responsibility"
[All syntax elements can be combined or nested using subpatterns.]
所有语法都可以使用子式样凑合或巢状回旋。

[Spammers]
滥发者
[Hello %sender%,\r\nI don't like such messages. Please don't send them to me anymore.\r\nThanks.\r\n\r\n(Automated message)]
您好 %sender%，\r\n我并不喜欢这种消息。请不要再传送给我了。\r\n谢谢。\r\n\r\n(自动消息)
[Hello %sender%,\r\nPlease reply "%securitycode%" if you want to contact me. If you don't reply correctly your messages will be ignored. Sorry for the inconvenience.\r\nThis spam check guarantees that you are a real person.\r\nYou have %triesleft% tries left.\r\nThanks in advance!\r\n\r\n(Automated message)]
您好 %sender%，\r\n如果您想联络我，请响应 "%securitycode%"。如果您没有正确地响应，您的消息将被忽略。我对任何导致的不方便致歉。\r\n此项滥发检查是用来确保您是真人。\r\n您还有 %triesleft% 次机会尝试。\r\n感谢您的合作！\r\n\r\n(自动消息)
[Thank you for your help!\r\nAll your previous messages were delivered. New messages do now reach me directly without an additional spam check.\r\n\r\n(Automated message)]
感谢您的协助！\r\n所有您之前的消息都已经递送。以后的消息也将直接接触我而不会经过附加的滥发检查。\r\n\r\n(自动消息)
[&Unmark spammer]
解除标示滥发者(&U)
[The entered phrase "%s" consists of a Regular Expression containing a syntax error!\r\n\r\nAdding an malformed Regular Expression will cause the filter\r\nto treat the expression as a normal phrase.\r\n\r\nShall the malformed Regular Expression be added anyway?]
您所输入的词汇 "%s" 包含了有错误的正规表示式！\r\n\r\n加入没有正确组成的正规表示式将令筛选器把表示式当作普通词汇。\r\n\r\n您仍然要加入这不正确组成的正规表示式？
[unlimited]
不限制
[The filter has detected %u malformed Regular Expression(s) in the default bad words!\r\n\r\nPlease update your installed Spam Definitions to the latest versions to resolve this problem.\r\nThis problem might also be caused by Spam Definitions that are not compatible with your system codepage.]
筛选器在预设的不当字词中侦测到 %u 个不正确组成的正规表示式！\r\n\r\n请更新您所安装的滥发定义到最新的版本以解决此问题。\r\n此问题亦可能是因滥发定义与您的系统代码页不兼容而导致的。
